    { 1100525006;1;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table11020225;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Year,Week,Header Project No.,Line No.)
                                 WHERE(Component Type=FILTER(Hours));
               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  Employee.CHANGECOMPANY("Supplying Company");
                                  IF NOT Employee.GET("Employee No.") THEN
                                    CLEAR(Employee); //in Case of Plant Hours

                                  EmplNameOtherCompany;

                                  DimensionManagement.GetDimValueRec(2, "Cost Object", DimensionValue, FALSE, "Project No.");

                                  IF PrintCompTotals THEN BEGIN
                                    CreateTempCompTotals("Wage Component", Monday, Tuesday, Wednesday, Thursday, Friday, Saturday, Sunday, "Total Line", 0);
                                    CalcCompTotal;
                                  END;

                                  IF "Cost Type" = "Cost Type"::Plant THEN BEGIN
                                    ProjPlantMonday := ProjPlantMonday + Monday;
                                    ProjPlantTuesday := ProjPlantTuesday + Tuesday;
                                    ProjPlantWednesday := ProjPlantWednesday + Wednesday;
                                    ProjPlantThursday := ProjPlantThursday + Thursday;
                                    ProjPlantFriday := ProjPlantFriday + Friday;
                                    ProjPlantSaturday := ProjPlantSaturday + Saturday;
                                    ProjPlantSunday := ProjPlantSunday + Sunday;
                                    ProjPlant := ProjPlant + "Total Line";
                                  END;

                                  HourAccountingProjectLineCount := HourAccountingProjectLineCount + 1;
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Year=FIELD(Year),
                            Week=FIELD(Week),
                            Header Project No.=FIELD(Project No.) }

    { 1100525009;;DataItem;ComponentTotals   ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number)
                                 WHERE(Number=FILTER(1..));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               TempHourAccountingProjectLine.RESET;

                               IF TempHourAccountingProjectLine.ISEMPTY THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;

                               SETRANGE(Number, 1, TempHourAccountingProjectLine.COUNT);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  Ok@1100525000 : Boolean;
                                BEGIN
                                  IF NOT PrintCompTotals THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF Number = 1 THEN
                                    Ok := TempHourAccountingProjectLine.FINDFIRST
                                  ELSE
                                    Ok := TempHourAccountingProjectLine.NEXT <> 0;
                                  IF NOT Ok THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF WageComponent.GET(TempHourAccountingProjectLine."Header Project No.") THEN
                                    WageComponentDescription := WageComponent.Description;
                                END;
                                 }

    PROCEDURE GetReportName@1100525003() : Text;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(DELSTR(CurrReport.OBJECTID, 1, STRPOS(CurrReport.OBJECTID, ' ')));
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetReportFilter@1100525000() : Text;
    BEGIN
      IF "Hour Accounting Project".GETFILTERS <> '' THEN
        EXIT(STRSUBSTNO('%1: %2', "Hour Accounting Project".TABLECAPTION, "Hour Accounting Project".GETFILTERS));
    END;

    PROCEDURE CreateTempCompTotals@11012006(Comp@11012000 : Code[10];Monday@1000000000 : Decimal;Tuesday@1000000001 : Decimal;Wednesday@1000000002 : Decimal;Thursday@1000000003 : Decimal;Friday@1000000004 : Decimal;Saturday@1000000005 : Decimal;Sunday@1000000006 : Decimal;Total@11012001 : Decimal;Amount@1210190000 : Decimal);
    BEGIN
      TempHourAccountingProjectLine.SETRANGE("Header Project No.", Comp);
      IF NOT TempHourAccountingProjectLine.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
        TempHourAccountingProjectLine.INIT;
        TempHourAccountingProjectLine."Header Project No." := Comp;
        TempHourAccountingProjectLine.Monday := Monday;
        TempHourAccountingProjectLine.Tuesday := Tuesday;
        TempHourAccountingProjectLine.Wednesday := Wednesday;
        TempHourAccountingProjectLine.Thursday := Thursday;
        TempHourAccountingProjectLine.Friday := Friday;
        TempHourAccountingProjectLine.Saturday := Saturday;
        TempHourAccountingProjectLine.Sunday := Sunday;
        TempHourAccountingProjectLine."Total Line" := Total;
        TempHourAccountingProjectLine."Amount (LCY)" := Amount;
        TempHourAccountingProjectLine.INSERT;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        TempHourAccountingProjectLine.Monday := TempHourAccountingProjectLine.Monday + Monday;
        TempHourAccountingProjectLine.Tuesday := TempHourAccountingProjectLine.Tuesday + Tuesday;
        TempHourAccountingProjectLine.Wednesday := TempHourAccountingProjectLine.Wednesday + Wednesday;
        TempHourAccountingProjectLine.Thursday := TempHourAccountingProjectLine.Thursday + Thursday;
        TempHourAccountingProjectLine.Friday := TempHourAccountingProjectLine.Friday + Friday;
        TempHourAccountingProjectLine.Saturday := TempHourAccountingProjectLine.Saturday + Saturday;
        TempHourAccountingProjectLine.Sunday := TempHourAccountingProjectLine.Sunday + Sunday;
        TempHourAccountingProjectLine."Total Line" := TempHourAccountingProjectLine."Total Line" + Total;
        TempHourAccountingProjectLine."Amount (LCY)" := TempHourAccountingProjectLine."Amount (LCY)" + Amount;
        TempHourAccountingProjectLine.MODIFY;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalcCompTotal@1000000002();
    BEGIN
      IF "Hour Accounting Project Line"."Cost Type" = "Hour Accounting Project Line"."Cost Type"::Plant THEN BEGIN
        TotPlantMonday := TotPlantMonday + "Hour Accounting Project Line".Monday;
        TotPlantTuesday := TotPlantTuesday + "Hour Accounting Project Line".Tuesday;
        TotPlantWednesday := TotPlantWednesday + "Hour Accounting Project Line".Wednesday;
        TotPlantThursday := TotPlantThursday + "Hour Accounting Project Line".Thursday;
        TotPlantFriday := TotPlantFriday + "Hour Accounting Project Line".Friday;
        TotPlantSaturday := TotPlantSaturday + "Hour Accounting Project Line".Saturday;
        TotPlantSunday := TotPlantSunday + "Hour Accounting Project Line".Sunday;
        TotPlant := TotPlant + "Hour Accounting Project Line"."Total Line";
        EXIT;
      END;

      IF NOT "Hour Accounting Project Line".Overtime THEN BEGIN
        TotNMonday := TotNMonday + "Hour Accounting Project Line".Monday;
        TotNTuesday := TotNTuesday + "Hour Accounting Project Line".Tuesday;
        TotNWednesday := TotNWednesday + "Hour Accounting Project Line".Wednesday;
        TotNThursday := TotNThursday + "Hour Accounting Project Line".Thursday;
        TotNFriday := TotNFriday + "Hour Accounting Project Line".Friday;
        TotNSaturday := TotNSaturday + "Hour Accounting Project Line".Saturday;
        TotNSunday := TotNSunday + "Hour Accounting Project Line".Sunday;
        TotN := TotN + "Hour Accounting Project Line"."Total Line";
      END ELSE BEGIN
        TotOMonday := TotOMonday + "Hour Accounting Project Line".Monday;
        TotOTuesday := TotOTuesday + "Hour Accounting Project Line".Tuesday;
        TotOWednesday := TotOWednesday + "Hour Accounting Project Line".Wednesday;
        TotOThursday := TotOThursday + "Hour Accounting Project Line".Thursday;
        TotOFriday := TotOFriday + "Hour Accounting Project Line".Friday;
        TotOSaturday := TotOSaturday + "Hour Accounting Project Line".Saturday;
        TotOSunday := TotOSunday + "Hour Accounting Project Line".Sunday;
        TotO := TotO + "Hour Accounting Project Line"."Total Line";
      END;
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
